  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>Hi <a href="https://issues.apache.org/jira/secure/ViewProfile.jspa?name=david.wright%40bksv.com" class="user-hover" rel="david.wright@bksv.com">David Wright</a>,</p> 
                  <p>I would like to propose to extends the GeoShape interfaces to be able to copy/serialized the objects. The current status and propose change is as following:</p> 
                  <p>GeoPoint: It can be serialized by using x, y, z<br> GeoCircle: It can be serialized by using getCenter() and getRadius() and getPlanetModel()<br> GeoCompositeShape: It can be serialized by accesing shapes using size() and GetShape(int index)<br> GeoPath: add methods to the interface getPoints() and getCutoffAngle()<br> GeoPolygon: This is the most complicated one as we have different types:<br> 1.- GeoCompositePolygon is just a composite<br> 2.- GeoConcavePolygon and GeoConvexPolygon: Create a new interface for those polygons which exposes the points, holes, internaledges and concavity/convexity<br> 3.- GeoComplexPolygons: Do nothing, they are too complex to be serialize??</p> 
                  <p>I am intersested in accesing the discreatization of the polygons into convex and concave ones for other reasons as well. I think this should be expose as they end result can be used for other use cases.</p> 
                  <p>Cheers,</p> 
                  <p>I.</p> 
                 </div> 
                </div> 
               </div>
              </div>

\u003cspan class=\'commentdate_16135074_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'21\\/Aug\\/17 11:54\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2017-08-21T11:54:03+0000\'\u003e21\\/Aug\\/17 11:54\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eCopying objects is not the main use case, what I want to achieve is what Spatial4j does with the binarycodec:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\\\"https:\\/\\/github.com\\/locationtech\\/spatial4j\\/blob\\/master\\/src\\/main\\/java\\/org\\/locationtech\\/spatial4j\\/io\\/BinaryCodec.java\\\" class=\\\"external-link\\\" rel=\\\"nofollow\\\"\u003ehttps:\\/\\/github.com\\/locationtech\\/spatial4j\\/blob\\/master\\/src\\/main\\/java\\/org\\/locationtech\\/spatial4j\\/io\\/BinaryCodec.java\u003c\\/a\u003e\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThis class is used to generate docValues which at the same time is used by the SerializedDVStrategy to check the relationship between indexed and query shapes. If we achieve this, we can pass through the interfaces the Geo3dShapes and use it with Lucene (I have already done it with very promising results). \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eIt is true that the objects can provide the methods to searialize\\/ deserialize but I thought Geoshapes should not need to know how to do this.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe second use case is the following: I am using healpix (\u003ca href=\\\"http:\\/\\/healpix.jpl.nasa.gov\\\" class=\\\"external-link\\\" rel=\\\"nofollow\\\"\u003ehttp:\\/\\/healpix.jpl.nasa.gov\u003c\\/a\u003e) to pixelate polygons on the sphere. The library requires polygons to be convex  therefore for concave polygons I need to break them into the equivalent convex ones, which is what the GeoPolygonFactory actually does. \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_16136663_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'22\\/Aug\\/17 11:32\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2017-08-22T11:32:01+0000\'\u003e22\\/Aug\\/17 11:32\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=ivera\\\" class=\\\"user-hover\\\" rel=\\\"ivera\\\"\u003eIgnacio Vera\u003c\\/a\u003e, thanks for the code patches.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI think we need to involve \u003ca href=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=dsmiley\\\" class=\\\"user-hover\\\" rel=\\\"dsmiley\\\"\u003eDavid Smiley\u003c\\/a\u003e if you want to extend what\'s in spatial-extras; he\'s the primary author of that module.  David, what is your opinion as to the spatial4j patch proposed?\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eAs for the binary codec, I\'ll have to think about how best to structure this.  Usually, as I\'ve indicated, it\'s better for packages structured as interfaces with multiple implementations to have each object know how to pack itself and unpack itself, rather than supporting deep inspection and writing a wrapper.  Too much internal information has to be exposed to do the latter.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI can see adding basic methods to all Geo3D objects for encoding to, and decoding from, a codec binary stream.  As long as these methods can be written efficiently, and the streams they read from\\/write to are standard in Lucene core or in the Java util package, I see no reason not to make this a standard feature of Geo3d.  A typical pattern would look something like this:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cdiv class=\\\"code panel\\\" style=\\\"border-width: 1px;\\\"\u003e\u003cdiv class=\\\"codeContent panelContent\\\"\u003e\\n\u003cpre class=\\\"code-java\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"code-keyword\\\"\u003epublic\u003c\\/span\u003e MyObject(\u003cspan class=\\\"code-keyword\\\"\u003efinal\u003c\\/span\u003e InputStream is) \u003cspan class=\\\"code-keyword\\\"\u003ethrows\u003c\\/span\u003e IOException {\\n  ...\\n}\\n\\n...\\n\\n@Override\\n\u003cspan class=\\\"code-keyword\\\"\u003epublic\u003c\\/span\u003e void write(\u003cspan class=\\\"code-keyword\\\"\u003efinal\u003c\\/span\u003e OutputStream os) \u003cspan class=\\\"code-keyword\\\"\u003ethrows\u003c\\/span\u003e IOException {\\n  ...\\n}\\n\\n\u003c\\/pre\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eTo be fully general, the interface-implementing class name would need to be included in the stream, and instantiated by reflection when the stream is read back.  This uses a fair bit of space but for your purposes might well be OK.  Please let me know.  I\'ll think on this further.\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"kwright@metacarta.com\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_16136663_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=kwright%40metacarta.com\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"kwright@metacarta.com\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Karl Wright\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_16136663_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'22\\/Aug\\/17 11:32\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2017-08-22T11:32:01+0000\'\u003e22\\/Aug\\/17 11:32\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                     Ignacio Vera , thanks for the code patches. \\n\\n I think we need to involve  David Smiley  if you want to extend what\'s in spatial-extras; he\'s the primary author of that module.  David, what is your opinion as to the spatial4j patch proposed? \\n\\n As for the binary codec, I\'ll have to think about how best to structure this.  Usually, as I\'ve indicated, it\'s better for packages structured as interfaces with multiple implementations to have each object know how to pack itself and unpack itself, rather than supporting deep inspection and writing a wrapper.  Too much internal information has to be exposed to do the latter. \\n\\n I can see adding basic methods to all Geo3D objects for encoding to, and decoding from, a codec binary stream.  As long as these methods can be written efficiently, and the streams they read from\\/write to are standard in Lucene core or in the Java util package, I see no reason not to make this a standard feature of Geo3d.  A typical pattern would look something like this: \\n\\n  \\n  public  MyObject( final  InputStream is)  throws  IOException {\\n  ...\\n}\\n\\n...\\n\\n@Override\\n public  void write( final  OutputStream os)  throws  IOException {\\n  ...\\n}\\n\\n \\n  \\n\\n To be fully general, the interface-implementing class name would need to be included in the stream, and instantiated by reflection when the stream is read back.  This uses a fair bit of space but for your purposes might well be OK.  Please let me know.  I\'ll think on this further.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-16136774\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/LUCENE-7936?focusedCommentId=16136774&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-16136774\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"ivera\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_16136774_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=ivera\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"ivera\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Ignacio Vera\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - My point is the following: \\n\\n There are basically two type of Objects for building shapes: \\n\\n GeoShape components: Everything that is extending the Vector class, GeoPoint and Planes. These do not need to be serialized. \\nGeoshape objects: Everything that  implements PlanetObject and hence extends GeoBasePanetObject. The interface PlanetObject should be implementing the SerializeObject. \\n\\n There should be no Geoshape extending GeoPoint as that is like trying to build a shape by extending a Plane. A GeoShapePoint object should be a GeoShapeObject with one component, being that component a GeoPoint. \\n\\n In addition, your  static methods to support serialization\\/deserialization  should live in GeoBasePanetObject. Then you can have them protected in the package. \\n\\n Cheers, \\n\\n I. \\n\\n             \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n They do not include the planet model.  In fact, no serialization yet includes the planet model; it is implied and included as an argument. But you are correct that readObject and writeObject should be made so.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThanks!\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"kwright@metacarta.com\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_16141458_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=kwright%40metacarta.com\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"kwright@metacarta.com\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Karl Wright\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_16141458_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'25\\/Aug\\/17 10:23\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2017-08-25T10:23:34+0000\'\u003e25\\/Aug\\/17 10:23\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                     Ignacio Vera , thanks for the patch. \\n\\n (1) GeoPoints serialize as two doubles. I think we should explore that option. \\n\\n I am attaching a factory that codifies the class into a byte. 0 to 127 is reserve for internal classes and -128 to -1 to user define classes. To make this work for objects that serialize other objects we would need to pass the factory into the constructor.  \\n\\n Anyway before going to details I want to check if you are ok to explore other solutions. class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2017-08-29T10:09:30+0000\'\u003e29\\/Aug\\/17 10:09\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=ivera\\\" class=\\\"user-hover\\\" rel=\\\"ivera\\\"\u003eIgnacio Vera\u003c\\/a\u003e, I committed the missing constructor.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI had thought that we eventually could improve the packing of class names.  However, to be a correct implementation, this needs to be built into SerializableObject fully, since there are a number of objects which decompose heterogeneously into subobjects.  I would therefore want to see the patch restructured to modify SerializableObject in that way.  The problem, of course, is that you need an object that you instantiate somehow that drives the serialization and deserialization, and the SerializableObject API is not set up to use such a thing.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eInstead, these are your options:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e(1) Have a static table of standard classes and a class-name encoding that starts with a byte.  If the byte is not 0xff, then look up the standard class from the table.  If not, follow the byte with the string encoding we do right now.  Works fine in a static environment, but custom classes are more expensive to serialize.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e(2) Have a non-static \\\"SerializationContext\\\" class that you initialize before you serialize or deserialize.  Then, every write() or deserialization construct must get the SerializationContext passed as an argument.  SerializationObject.readObject() and SerializationObject.writeObject() must also receive this parameter.  This is a major bit of work, of course, but might be worth it if you intend to do lots of custom geo classes.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eOne other comment on code: I notice you throw some RuntimeExceptions.  Those are inappropriate for bad arguments or a bad object state.  Use IllegalArgumentException or IllegalStateException instead in those cases.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003ePlease let me know what you want to do.\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"kwright@metacarta.com\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_16145047_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=kwright%40metacarta.com\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"kwright@metacarta.com\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Karl Wright\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_16145047_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'29\\/Aug\\/17 10:09\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2017-08-29T10:09:30+0000\'\u003e29\\/Aug\\/17 10:09\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                     Ignacio Vera , I committed the missing constructor. \\n\\n I had thought that we eventually could improve the packing of class names.  However, to be a correct implementation, this needs to be built into SerializableObject fully, since there are a number of objects which decompose heterogeneously into subobjects.  I would therefore want to see the patch restructured to modify SerializableObject in that way.  The problem, of course, is that you need an object that you instantiate somehow that drives the serialization and deserialization, and the SerializableObject API is not set up to use such a thing. \\n\\n Instead, these are your options: \\n\\n (1) Have a static table of standard classes and a class-name encoding that starts with a byte.  If the byte is not 0xff, then look up the standard class from the table.  If not, follow the byte with the string encoding we do right now.  Works fine in a static environment, but custom classes are more expensive to serialize. \\n\\n (2) Have a non-static \\\"SerializationContext\\\" class that you initialize before you serialize or deserialize.  Then, every write() or deserialization construct must get the SerializationContext passed as an argument.  SerializationObject.readObject() and SerializationObject.writeObject() must also receive this parameter.  This is a major bit of work, of course, but might be worth it if you intend to do lots of custom geo classes. \\n\\n One other comment on code: I notice you throw some RuntimeExceptions.  Those are inappropriate for bad arguments or a bad object state.  Use IllegalArgumentException or IllegalStateException instead in those cases. \\n\\n Please let me know what you want to do.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n
